		e.preventDefault();
		$('.menu_gg li').removeClass('active');
		$(this).addClass('active');
		var gtype = $(this).data('t');
		$('.box_timkiem_gg_s form').attr('data-type', gtype);
	});
	$('.box_timkiem_gg_s form').submit(function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		if($(this).closest('form').find('input').val() == '') {
			alert('Chưa nhập từ khóa');
		} else {
			var act = 'https://www.google.com/search';
			var gtype = $('.box_timkiem_gg_s form').attr('data-type');
			var gsearch = $('#gkeywords').val().replace(' ', '+');
			if(gtype == 1) {
				act = act + '?q='+gsearch+'&udm=2';
				$('.box_timkiem_gg_s form').attr('action', act);
			}
			if(gtype == 2) {
				act = act + '?q='+gsearch+'&tbm=vid';
				$('.box_timkiem_gg_s form').attr('action', act);
			}
			if(gtype == 3) {
				act = act + '?q='+gsearch;
				$('.box_timkiem_gg_s form').attr('action', act);
			}
			if(gtype == 4) {
			var act = 'https://home.vn/tim-kiem//';
				act = act + '?q='+gsearch;
				$('.box_timkiem_gg_s form').attr('action', act);
				location.href=act;
				return false;
			}
			if(gtype == 5) {
				act = 'https://translate.google.com/?sl=auto&tl=en&text='+gsearch+'&op=translate';
				$('.box_timkiem_gg_s form').attr('action', act);
			}
			if(gtype == 6) {
				act = 'https://www.google.com/maps/search/'+gsearch;
				$('.box_timkiem_gg_s form').attr('action', act);
			}
			window.open(act, '_blank');
		}
	});

</script>

	navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(geoFunc, errFunc);
	var dcc = 'HH1, Yen Hoa, Cau Giay, Ha Noi, Yên Hoà, Cầu Giấy, Hà Nội, Vietnam';
	$('body').attr('data-latitude', 21.02185);

	function geoFunc(e){
		//console.log(e);
		var lati = e.coords.latitude;
		var loti = e.coords.longitude;
		var accu = e.coords.accuracy;
		$('body').attr('data-latitude', lati);
		$('body').attr('data-longitude', loti);
		homevn_weather('', lati+','+loti);
	}
	function errFunc(e){
		homevn_weather('Hà Nội');
		//console.log(e);
	}
	function homevn_weather(area, geo = ''){
		$('.menu--location').removeClass('is-active');
		$.getJSON("/metrics/thoitiet?area="+area+"&geo="+geo, function(bp) {
			//console.log(Math.round(bp.result.current.temp));
			$('a.p-navgroup-link.location span').text(bp.result.province);
			$('.p-nav-opposite .location').show();
			$('.lich-ngay .lich-tinh').html('<a href="/tien-ich/weather" data-xf-click="switch-overlay">'+$('.p-nav-opposite .location').html()+'</a>');
			var nhietdo = Math.round(bp.result.current.temp);
			if(nhietdo > 0) {
				var tinhtrang = bp.result.current.status;
				tinhtrang = tinhtrang.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase() + tinhtrang.substring(1, tinhtrang.length);
				var mayicon = bp.result.current.icon;
				const now = new Date();
				const hours = now.getHours().toString().padStart(2, '0');
				const currentHour = `${hours}:00`;
				const currentWeather = bp.result.hourly.find(item => item.title === currentHour);

				if (currentWeather) {
				  var nhietdo = Math.round(currentWeather.temp);
				  var tinhtrang = currentWeather.status;
				  var mayicon = currentWeather.icon;
				}

				var thap = Math.round(bp.result.current.min);
				var cao = Math.round(bp.result.current.max);
				$('.p-navgroup-link.weather').html('<span>'+nhietdo+'°C</span><span>'+tinhtrang+'</span><span><i class="far fa-long-arrow-alt-down" style="color:#58cbdc"></i> '+thap+' <i class="far fa-long-arrow-alt-up" style="color:#f44336"></i> '+cao+'</span>');
				var btuong = '<img src="/styles/homevn/weather/'+mayicon+'.png.svg" alt="'+bp.result.current.icon+'"  width="22">';
				$('.p-navgroup-link.location .may').html(btuong);
				$('.p-nav-opposite .location, .p-nav-opposite .weather').show();
				if($(window).width() <= 650) {
					var formb = '<div class="mbwther"><span><a href="/tien-ich/weather" data-xf-click="switch-overlay">'+$('.p-nav-opposite .location').html()+'</a></span><span><span>'+nhietdo+'°C</span>, <span>'+tinhtrang+'</span></span></div>';
					$('.p-body').prepend(formb);
				}
			}
		});
		return false;
	}
	function homevn_location(){
		$('.tinhthanh_list').html('');
		$.getJSON("/data/lat_long.json", function(jsons) {
			$.each(jsons,function(key,json){
				$('.tinhthanh_list').append('<li><a href="javascript:;" onClick="homevn_weather(\''+json.name+'\')">'+json.name+'</a></li>');
			});
		});
	}
	homevn_location();

</script>

$('a.reaction').click(function(e){ 
	var hrr = $(this).attr('href').split('/');
	var pidd = hrr[2];
	var baicl = $('.vp_'+pidd+':first .counter');
	if($('.vp_'+pidd+' .has-reaction').length > 0) {
		var tru = 1;
		if(parseInt(baicl.text()) > baicl.data('num')) var tru = 0;
		var pcu = parseInt(parseInt(baicl.data('num')) - tru);
		if(pcu < baicl.data('num') - 2) pcu = baicl.data('num') - 1;
	} else {
		var cong = 1;
		if(parseInt(baicl.text()) > baicl.data('num')) var cong = 0;
		var pcu = parseInt(parseInt(baicl.data('num')) + cong);
		if(pcu > baicl.data('num') + 2) pcu = baicl.data('num') + 1;
	}

	$('.vp_'+pidd+' .counter').text(pcu);
});

</script>
<script>

function timeAgo(unixTime) {
  const now = new Date();
  const then = new Date(unixTime * 1000);
  const diffSec = Math.floor((now - then) / 1000);

  const phrase = (key, count) => XF.phrase(`b_stat_${key}_ago`, { count });

  if (diffSec < 60) return b_stat_phrase('{count} giây trước', diffSec);
  if (diffSec < 3600) return b_stat_phrase('{count} phút trước', Math.floor(diffSec / 60));
  if (diffSec < 86400) return b_stat_phrase('{count} giờ trước', Math.floor(diffSec / 3600));
  if (diffSec < 2592000) return b_stat_phrase('{count} ngày trước', Math.floor(diffSec / 86400));

  const yearDiff = now.getFullYear() - then.getFullYear();
  const monthDiff = now.getMonth() - then.getMonth();
  let totalMonths = yearDiff * 12 + monthDiff;

  if (totalMonths < 12) return b_stat_phrase('{count} tháng trước', totalMonths);

  const years = Math.floor(totalMonths / 12);
  const months = totalMonths % 12;

  if (months === 0) return b_stat_phrase('{count} năm trước', years);
  return b_stat_phrase('{count} năm trước', years);
}
function b_stat_phrase(templatex, count) {
    count = Math.max(1, count);
    return templatex
        .replace('{count}', count)
        .replace("{s}", count == 1 ? '' : 's');
}	   
document.querySelectorAll('.b_time_ago').forEach(el => {
  const unix = parseInt(el.dataset.value, 10);
  if (!isNaN(unix)) {
    el.textContent = timeAgo(unix);
  }
});
document.querySelectorAll('.vnxf_beststatpro').forEach(container => {
    const key = container.dataset.widgetKey;
    if (!key) return;
    const outer = document.createElement('div');
    outer.className = 'vnxf_beststatpro_outer';
    const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
    wrapper.id = 'vnxf_beststatpro_' + key;
    const reload = document.createElement('span');
    reload.className = 'vnxf_beststatpro_reload';
    reload.dataset.key = key;
    reload.innerHTML = `<i class="fa--xf fas fa-sync" aria-hidden="true"></i>`;
    container.parentNode.insertBefore(outer, container);
    wrapper.appendChild(container); 
    outer.appendChild(reload);
    outer.appendChild(wrapper); 
});
document.querySelectorAll('.vnxf_beststatpro_reload').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
        event.preventDefault();

        const key = button.dataset.key;
        if (!key) return;

        const target = document.getElementById('vnxf_beststatpro_' + key);
        if (!target) return;
		const activeTab = target.querySelector('.tabs_tab_bsp.is-active');
		const activeHref = activeTab ? activeTab.getAttribute('data-id') : null;
		var acurl = '/misc/b-stat';
		XF.ajax("post", acurl, {'wkey': key, '_xfToken': '1771929690,ebf8a8987f0c7c1197f288d56f132874'}, function(data) {
                if (data.html && data.html.content) {
                        target.innerHTML = (data.html.content);  
						document.querySelectorAll('.b_time_ago').forEach(el => {
						  const unix = parseInt(el.dataset.value, 10);
						  if (!isNaN(unix)) {
							el.textContent = timeAgo(unix);
						  }
						});
					vnxf_beststatpro_change_tab();
					const tab = target.querySelector(`.tabs_tab_bsp[data-id="${activeHref}"]`);
					if (tab) tab.click();
                }
		});
	});
});
function vnxf_beststatpro_change_tab() {
  const tabHeaders = document.querySelectorAll(".vnxf_beststatpro .tabs_tab_bsp");
  tabHeaders.forEach(header => {
    header.addEventListener("click", function () {
      const container = header.closest(".vnxf_beststatpro");
      const tabId = '#'+header.dataset.id;

      if (!tabId) return;

      // Active tab headers
      const allTabs = container.querySelectorAll(".tabs_tab_bsp");
      allTabs.forEach(tab => tab.classList.remove("is-active"));
      header.classList.add("is-active");

      // Active tab panes
      const panes = container.querySelectorAll(".tabPanes_bsp > div");
      panes.forEach(pane => pane.classList.remove("is-active"));

      const activePane = container.querySelector(tabId);
      if (activePane) activePane.classList.add("is-active");
    });
  });
}
vnxf_beststatpro_change_tab();

</script>

	function gettimeAgo(unixTime) {
	  const now = new Date();
	  const then = new Date(unixTime * 1000);
	  const diffSec = Math.floor((now - then) / 1000);

	  const phrase = (key, count) => XF.phrase(`b_stat_${key}_ago`, { count });

	  if (diffSec < 60) return b_stat_phrase('{count} giây trước', diffSec);
	  if (diffSec < 3600) return b_stat_phrase('{count} phút trước', Math.floor(diffSec / 60));
	  if (diffSec < 86400) return b_stat_phrase('{count} giờ trước', Math.floor(diffSec / 3600));
	  if (diffSec < 2592000) return b_stat_phrase('{count} ngày trước', Math.floor(diffSec / 86400));

	  const yearDiff = now.getFullYear() - then.getFullYear();
	  const monthDiff = now.getMonth() - then.getMonth();
	  let totalMonths = yearDiff * 12 + monthDiff;

	  if (totalMonths < 12) return b_stat_phrase('{count} tháng trước', totalMonths);

	  const years = Math.floor(totalMonths / 12);
	  const months = totalMonths % 12;

	  if (months === 0) return t_phrase('{count} năm trước', years);
	  return t_phrase('{count} năm trước', years);
	}
	function t_phrase(templatex, count) {
		return templatex
			.replace('{count}', count)
			.replace("{s}", count == 1 ? '' : 's');
	}	   
	document.querySelectorAll('.time_ago').forEach(el => {
	  const unix = parseInt(el.dataset.value, 10);
	  if (!isNaN(unix)) {
		el.textContent = gettimeAgo(unix);
	  }
	});

</script>

	<script>
		function decodeJwtResponse(token) {
			var base64Url = token.split(".")[1];
			var base64 = base64Url.replace(/-/g, "+").replace(/_/g, "/");
			var jsonPayload = decodeURIComponent(
				atob(base64)
				.split("")
				.map(function (c) {
					return "%" + ("00" + c.charCodeAt(0).toString(16)).slice(-2);
				})
				.join("")
			);
			return (jsonPayload);
		}
